# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

- **OffsetMetadataManager** - Central manager for offset storage, retrieval, and deletion

### 2. **Request/Response Protocol Handlers**
- **OffsetCommitRequest/Response** - Protocol for committing offsets
- **OffsetFetchRequest/Response** - Protocol for retrieving offsets
- **OffsetDeleteRequest** - Protocol for deleting offsets

- **GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers** - Utilities for offset record serialization (including legacy format support)
- **ConsumerCoordinator/CommitRequestManager** - Client-side offset management
- **LogCleanerManager** - Handles offset expiry and compaction of __consumer_offsets topic

enables consumer groups to persist and retrieve committed offsets for topic partitions. The architecture spans multiple layers from protocol definitions to broker-side coordination.\\n\\n### Core Offset Storage\\n\\nThe `__consumer_offsets` internal topic is the central repository for all consumer group offset information. The OffsetAndMetadata class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetAndMetadata.java) serves as the server-side representation of committed offsets, storing the offset value, optional leader epoch, and custom metadata. This is complemented by the client-side OffsetAndMetadata class (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/OffsetAndMetadata.java) that consumers use to commit offsets.\\n\\n### GroupCoordinator Architecture\\n\\nThe GroupCoordinator interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) defines the contract for offset management operations. It's implemented by GroupCoordinatorService (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorService.java), which delegates to GroupCoordinatorShard instances for distributed coordination. The GroupCoordinatorShard (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java) manages in-memory state for specific topic partitions.\\n\\n### Offset Management Operations\\n\\n**Offset Commit Handler**: The OffsetMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java) is responsible for handling offset commits. It validates commit requests, updates offset state, and persists offset records to the __consumer_offsets topic. The GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.java) provides utilities for creating and converting offset commit records, including legacy format support.\\n\\n**Offset Fetch Handler**: When clients request to fetch committed offsets, the OffsetMetadataManager's fetchOffsets method retrieves the stored offsets from its in-memory state. The fetchOffsets operation in GroupCoordinatorShard coordinates the retrieval and formats responses according to the protocol version.\\n\\n**Offset Deletion**: The deleteOffsets method in OffsetMetadataManager handles offset deletion requests, creating tombstone records for offset keys to remove them during log compaction.\\n\\n### Request/Response Protocol\\n\\nThe OffsetCommitRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetCommitRequest.java) and OffsetCommitResponse (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetCommitResponse.java) classes handle the protocol for committing offsets. Similarly, OffsetFetchRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchRequest.java) and OffsetFetchResponse (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchResponse.java) handle offset retrieval, and OffsetDeleteRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetDeleteRequest.java) supports offset deletion via the admin API.\\n\\n### Broker-Side Request Handling\\n\\nThe KafkaApis.scala file (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaApis.scala) contains the broker-level handlers: handleOffsetCommitRequest, handleOffsetFetchRequest, and handleOffsetDeleteRequest. These handlers parse protocol requests, perform authorization checks, and delegate to the GroupCoordinator for actual offset operations.\\n\\n### Client-Side Offset Management\\n\\nThe ConsumerCoordinator (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ConsumerCoordinator.java) manages offset commit operations on the consumer side. The CommitRequestManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CommitRequestManager.java) handles queueing and retrying of offset commit requests. The OffsetCommitCallbackInvoker (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/OffsetCommitCallbackInvoker.java) invokes user callbacks upon successful offset commits.\\n\\n### Group Types and Offset Management\\n\\nBoth ClassicGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java) and ConsumerGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java) implement the Group interface and support offset management operations. The GroupMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java) manages group membership state and coordinates with the OffsetMetadataManager for offset operations.\\n\\n### Offset Expiry and Compaction\\n\\nOffsets are automatically expired based on retention policy configured in GroupCoordinatorConfig (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorConfig.java). The LogCleanerManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogCleanerManager.java) handles log compaction of the __consumer_offsets topic, removing expired offset records via tombstones.\\n\\n### Metrics and Monitoring\\n\\nThe GroupCoordinatorMetrics (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/metrics/GroupCoordinatorMetrics.java) and GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/metrics/GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard.java) track offset commit operations. The OffsetCommitMetricsManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/metrics/OffsetCommitMetricsManager.java) provides client-side metrics for offset commit performance.\\n\\n### Admin Operations\\n\\nThe DeleteConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/admin/internals/DeleteConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler.java) and ListConsumerGroupOffsetsResult (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/admin/ListConsumerGroupOffsetsResult.java) support administrative operations for deleting and listing consumer group offsets.\\n\"\n}\n",

\"addOffsetCommitRequest\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"## Consumer Offset Management Architecture in Apache Kafka\\n\\nApache Kafka implements a sophisticated consumer offset management system that enables consumer groups to persist and retrieve committed offsets for topic partitions. The architecture spans multiple layers from protocol definitions to broker-side coordination.\\n\\n### Core Offset Storage\\n\\nThe `__consumer_offsets` internal topic is the central repository for all consumer group offset information. The OffsetAndMetadata class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetAndMetadata.java) serves as the server-side representation of committed offsets, storing the offset value, optional leader epoch, and custom metadata. This is complemented by the client-side OffsetAndMetadata class (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/OffsetAndMetadata.java) that consumers use to commit offsets.\\n\\n### GroupCoordinator Architecture\\n\\nThe GroupCoordinator interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) defines the contract for offset management operations. It's implemented by GroupCoordinatorService (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorService.java), which delegates to GroupCoordinatorShard instances for distributed coordination. The GroupCoordinatorShard (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java) manages in-memory state for specific topic partitions.\\n\\n### Offset Management Operations\\n\\n**Offset Commit Handler**: The OffsetMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java) is responsible for handling offset commits. It validates commit requests, updates offset state, and persists offset records to the __consumer_offsets topic. The GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.java) provides utilities for creating and converting offset commit records, including legacy format support.\\n\\n**Offset Fetch Handler**: When clients request to fetch committed offsets, the OffsetMetadataManager's fetchOffsets method retrieves the stored offsets from its in-memory state. The fetchOffsets operation in GroupCoordinatorShard coordinates the retrieval and formats responses according to the protocol version.\\n\\n**Offset Deletion**: The deleteOffsets method in OffsetMetadataManager handles offset deletion requests, creating tombstone records for offset keys to remove them during log compaction.\\n\\n### Request/Response Protocol\\n\\nThe OffsetCommitRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetCommitRequest.java) and OffsetCommitResponse (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetCommitResponse.java) classes handle the protocol for committing offsets. Similarly, OffsetFetchRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchRequest.java) and OffsetFetchResponse (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetFetchResponse.java) handle offset retrieval, and OffsetDeleteRequest (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/OffsetDeleteRequest.java) supports offset deletion via the admin API.\\n\\n### Broker-Side Request Handling\\n\\nThe KafkaApis.scala file (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaApis.scala) contains the broker-level handlers: handleOffsetCommitRequest, handleOffsetFetchRequest, and handleOffsetDeleteRequest. These handlers parse protocol requests, perform authorization checks, and delegate to the GroupCoordinator for actual offset operations.\\n\\n### Client-Side Offset Management\\n\\nThe ConsumerCoordinator (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ConsumerCoordinator.java) manages offset commit operations on the consumer side. The CommitRequestManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CommitRequestManager.java) handles queueing and retrying of offset commit requests. The OffsetCommitCallbackInvoker (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/OffsetCommitCallbackInvoker.java) invokes user callbacks upon successful offset commits.\\n\\n### Group Types and Offset Management\\n\\nBoth ClassicGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java) and ConsumerGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java) implement the Group interface and support offset management operations. The GroupMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java) manages group membership state and coordinates with the OffsetMetadataManager for offset operations.\\n\\n### Offset Expiry and Compaction\\n\\nOffsets are automatically expired based on retention policy configured in GroupCoordinatorConfig (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorConfig.java). The LogCleanerManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogCleanerManager.java) handles log compaction of the __consumer_offsets topic, removing expired offset records via tombstones.\\n\\n### Metrics and Monitoring\\n\\nThe GroupCoordinatorMetrics (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/metrics/GroupCoordinatorMetrics.java) and GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/metrics/GroupCoordinatorMetricsShard.java) track offset commit operations. The OffsetCommitMetricsManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/metrics/OffsetCommitMetricsManager.java) provides client-side metrics for offset commit performance.\\n\\n### Admin Operations\\n\\nThe DeleteConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/admin/internals/DeleteConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler.java) and ListConsumerGroupOffsetsResult (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/admin/ListConsumerGroupOffsetsResult.java) support administrative operations for deleting and listing consumer group offsets.\\n\"\n}\n",
